Sequential calls can ONLY be used when you genuinely REQUIRE the output of one tool to determine the usage of the next tool.\n\nDEFAULT TO PARALLEL: Unless you have a specific reason why operations MUST be sequential (output of A required for input of B), always execute multiple tools simultaneously. This is not just an optimization - it's the expected behavior. authentication schemes\n- **Core component attribute definitions**: When describing properties, types, default values, and behaviors of key UI components, services, or configuration objects\n- **Database table schemas**: When outlining tables, columns, data types, constraints (PK, FK, unique), indexes, and relationships between entities\n- **Configuration options**: When listing environment variables, feature flags, or system settings with descriptions, valid values, and scope\n- **State or enum definitions**: When clarifying possible states, status codes, or enumerated values used across the system\n- **Input/output specifications**: When defining the structure of data inputs (forms, payloads) or expected outputs (reports, responses) for clarity and validation\n- **Migration or version changes**: When comparing changes across versions, such as deprecated fields, added endpoints, or schema evolution\n\n## 7. Error\"]\n    DBResult --\u003e|Yes| ProcessData[\"Process Raw Data\"]\n    ProcessData --\u003e UpdateCache[\"Update Cache\"]\n    UpdateCache --\u003e ReturnResult[\"Return Processed Result\"]\n    HandleError --\u003e ReturnError\n    ReturnCache --\u003e End([Function Exit])\n    ReturnResult --\u003e End\n    ReturnError --\u003e End\n```\n\n## Architecture Diagrams\n```mermaid\ngraph TB\n uuid id PK\n    string name\n    string description\n    uuid owner_id FK\n    timestamp created_at\n    timestamp updated_at\n    enum status\n  }\n\n  TASK {\n    uuid id PK\n    string title\n    text description\n    uuid project_id FK\n    uuid assignee_id FK\n    timestamp due_date\n    enum priority\n    enum status\n  }\n\n  USER ||--o{ PROJECT : owns\n  USER ||--o{ TASK : assigned_to\n  PROJECT ||--o{ TASK : contains\n```\n\n## Common Mermaid Syntax Errors to Avoid:\n\n### WRONG - Custom Colors and Styling\n```\nclassDiagram\n    class User {\n        name: string\n    }\n  A[Complex Label With Spaces] --\u003e B\n```\n\n### CORRECT - Quoted Labels\n```mermaid\nflowchart TD\n    A[\"Complex Label With Spaces\"] --\u003e B[\"Another Label\"]\n```\n\n# FINAL DOCUMENT Core Functionality and Services Identification\\nPrincipal features:\\n- Multilingual support (Arabic, English, Turkish) with RTL layout for Arabic\\n- Event information display (date, time, location)\\n- Agenda section with event schedule\\n- Speakers section with participant information\\n- Goals and purpose of the event\\n- Organizers information\\n- Registration section\\n- Responsive design with mobile support\\n- Internationalization system with language context\\n\\n5. Codebase Deep Dive\\nCritical code modules:\\n- LanguageContext.tsx: Manages multilingual functionality with translation system and RTL support\\n- App.tsx: Root application component with providers for routing, internationalization, and state management\\n- Index.tsx: Main page component that composes all sections\\n- eventData.ts: Central data model for event information\\n- ui/ components: ShadCN UI library components built on Radix UI primitives\\n\\nArchitectural patterns:\\n- Component-based architecture with React\\n- Context API for global state management (language, theme)\\n- Atomic design principles in UI components\\n- Custom hooks for reusable logic (use-mobile, use-toast)\\n- Provider pattern for dependency injection\\n\\n6. Feature Hierarchy/Mapping\\n- Core Application\\n  - Internationalization\\n    - Language switching (ar, en, tr)\\n    - RTL layout support\\n    - Translation system\\n  - Responsive Design\\n    - Mobile detection\\n    - Adaptive layouts\\n  - Navigation\\n    - Navbar with language switcher\\n    - Scroll-to-top functionality\\n  - Event Information\\n    - Hero section\\n    - Countdown timer\\n    - Details section (date, time, location)\\n    - Why section (event purpose)\\n    - Goals section\\n    - Agenda section\\n    - Speakers section\\n    - Organizers section\\n    - Registration section\\n    - Footer\\n\\n7. Beginner-Friendly Guidance\\nConcepts requiring detailed explanation:\\n- React Context API for state management\\n- Internationalization implementation with translation functions\\n- ShadCN UI component library usage\\n- Tailwind CSS utility-first styling approach\\n- Vite build tool configuration\\n- TypeScript interfaces and types\\n\\nPrerequisite knowledge:\\n- Basic React concepts (components, hooks, JSX)\\n- TypeScript fundamentals\\n- CSS and responsive design principles\\n- Understanding of modern JavaScript (ES6+)\\n- Familiarity with npm package management\\n\\n8. Code Structure Analysis\\nCode structure patterns:\\n- Component composition pattern\\n- Context-based state management\\n- Custom hooks for reusable logic\\n- Separation of concerns between UI components and business logic\\n\\nComponent relationships:\\n- App component wraps all providers (QueryClient, LanguageProvider, TooltipProvider)\\n- Index page imports and composes all section components\\n- Section components use UI components from the ui/ directory\\n- LanguageContext provides translation function (t) and language state to all components\\n\\n9. Data Flow Analysis\\nData pathways:\\n- LanguageContext provides language state and translation function to all components\\n- eventData.ts provides event data to components\\n- Translation system flows from LanguageContext to individual components via the t() function\\n- User interactions (language selection) update context state which propagates to all components\\n\\nCritical data models:\\n- LanguageContextType: Defines the structure of the language context\\n- eventData: Central data object containing all event information\\n- Speaker interface: Defines speaker data structure\\n\\n10. Integration and Extension Points Identification\\nExtension mechanisms:\\n- Language system can be extended with additional languages\\n- Event data can be modified or loaded from external sources\\n- UI components can be customized through Tailwind configuration\\n- Theme can be extended with additional color schemes\\n\\nIntegration points:\\n- Google Maps integration for venue location\\n- Potential registration system integration\\n- Social media sharing capabilities\\n- Analytics integration\\n\\n11. Dependency Analysis\\nExternal dependencies:\\n- React and React DOM: Core UI library\\n- Vite: Build tool and development server\\n- Tailwind CSS: Styling framework\\n- ShadCN UI: Component library built on Radix UI\\n- React Router DOM: Client-side routing\\n- React Query: Data fetching and caching\\n- date-fns: Date manipulation utilities\\n- lucide-react: Icon library\\n\\nInternal component interdependencies:\\n- App depends on all section components and providers\\n- Section components depend on UI components and hooks\\n- UI components depend on utility functions (cn)\\n- All components depend on LanguageContext for translations\\n\\n12. User Workflow Mapping\\nCommon user scenarios:\\n1. User visits site â†’ Language selection â†’ Views event information in selected language\\n2. User navigates through event sections using navbar or scrolling\\n3. User views event details (date, time, location) and clicks to view on map\\n4. User explores agenda, speakers, and organizers\\n5. User registers for event through registration section\\n6. User switches languages at any point to view content in preferred language\\n\\nKey entry points:\\n- Main page (Index) as primary entry point\\n- Direct links to specific sections (agenda, speakers, etc.)\\n- Language switcher for immediate language selection\\n\\n13. Code Structure Analysis\\nCode structure patterns:\\n- Component composition pattern\\n- Context-based state management\\n- Custom hooks for reusable logic\\n- Separation of concerns between UI components and business logic\\n\\nComponent relationships:\\n- App component wraps all providers (QueryClient, LanguageProvider, TooltipProvider)\\n- Index page imports and composes all section components\\n- Section components use UI components from the ui/ directory\\n- LanguageContext provides translation function (t) and language state to all components\\n\\n9. Data Flow Analysis\\nData pathways:\\n- LanguageContext provides language state and translation function to all components\\n- eventData.ts provides event data to components\\n- Translation system flows from LanguageContext to individual components via the t() function\\n- User interactions (language selection) update context state which propagates to all components\\n\\nCritical data models:\\n- LanguageContextType: Defines the structure of the language context\\n- eventData: Central data object containing all event information\\n- Speaker interface: Defines speaker data structure\\n\\n10. Integration and Extension Points Identification\\nExtension mechanisms:\\n- Language system can be extended with additional languages\\n- Event data can be modified or loaded from external sources\\n- UI components can be customized through Tailwind configuration\\n- Theme can be extended with additional color schemes\\n\\nIntegration points:\\n- Google Maps integration for venue location\\n- Potential registration system integration\\n- Social media sharing capabilities\\n- Analytics integration\\n\\n11. Dependency Analysis\\nExternal dependencies:\\n- React and React DOM: Core UI library\\n- Vite: Build tool and development server\\n- Tailwind CSS: Styling framework\\n- ShadCN UI: Component library built on Radix UI\\n- React Router DOM: Client-side routing\\n- React Query: Data fetching and caching\\n- date-fns: Date manipulation utilities\\n- lucide-react: Icon library\\n\\nInternal component interdependencies:\\n- App depends on all section components and providers\\n- Section components depend on UI components and hooks\\n- UI components depend on utility functions (cn)\\n- All components depend on LanguageContext for translations\\n\\n12. User Workflow Mapping\\nCommon user scenarios:\\n1. User visits site â†’ Language selection â†’ Views event information in selected language\\n2. User navigates through event sections using navbar or scrolling\\n3. User views event details (date, time, location) and clicks to view on map\\n4. User explores agenda, speakers, and organizers\\n5. User registers for event through registration section\\n6. User switches languages at any point to view content in preferred language\\n\\nKey entry points:\\n- Main page (Index) as primary entry point\\n- Direct links to specific sections (agenda, speakers, etc.)\\n- Language switcher for immediate language selection\\n\\n13. The application is designed as a multilingual event platform for the Syrian community, featuring responsive design and internationalization support.\\n\\n2. Codebase Overview/Analysis\\n- Core functionality: A multilingual event website for the Syrian community with event details, agenda, speakers, registration, and organizational information.\\n- Primary use cases: Displaying event information in Arabic, English, and Turkish with RTL support for Arabic.\\n- Primary programming languages: TypeScript, JSX, CSS (via Tailwind)\\n- Critical frameworks and library dependencies:\\n  - React 18 with TypeScript\\n  - Vite as build tool\\n  - Tailwind CSS for styling\\n  - ShadCN UI components built on Radix UI primitives\\n  - React Router DOM for routing\\n  - React Query for data management\\n  - date-fns for date manipulation\\n\\n3. Project Directory Architecture Mapping/Analysis\\n- src/: Main source code directory\\n  - components/: Reusable UI components including ShadCN UI library components and custom application components\\n  - data/: Event data and content\\n  - hooks/: Custom React hooks\\n  - lib/: Utility functions\\n  - pages/: Application pages\\n- public/: Static assets and manifest files\\n- Configuration files:\\n  - package.json: Project metadata and dependencies\\n  - vite.config.ts: Vite build configuration\\n  - tailwind.config.ts: Tailwind CSS customization\\n  - tsconfig.json: TypeScript configuration\\n  - eslint.config.js: ESLint configuration\\n\\n4. Core Functionality and Services Identification\\nPrincipal features:\\n- Multilingual support (Arabic, English, Turkish) with RTL layout for Arabic\\n- Event information display (date, time, location)\\n- Agenda section with event schedule\\n- Speakers section with participant information\\n- Goals and purpose of the event\\n- Organizers information\\n- Registration section\\n- Responsive design with mobile support\\n- Internationalization system with language context\\n\\n5. Codebase Deep Dive\\nCritical code modules:\\n- LanguageContext.tsx: Manages multilingual functionality with translation system and RTL support\\n- App.tsx: Root application component with providers for routing, internationalization, and state management\\n- Index.tsx: Main page component that composes all sections\\n- eventData.ts: Central data model for event information\\n- ui/ components: ShadCN UI library components built on Radix UI primitives\\n\\nArchitectural patterns:\\n- Component-based architecture with React\\n- Context API for global state management (language, theme)\\n- Atomic design principles in UI components\\n- Custom hooks for reusable logic (use-mobile, use-toast)\\n- Provider pattern for dependency injection\\n\\n6. Feature Hierarchy/Mapping\\n- Core Application\\n  - Internationalization\\n    - Language switching (ar, en, tr)\\n    - RTL layout support\\n    - Translation system\\n  - Responsive Design\\n    - Mobile detection\\n    - Adaptive layouts\\n  - Navigation\\n    - Navbar with language switcher\\n    - Scroll-to-top functionality\\n  - Event Information\\n    - Hero section\\n    - Countdown timer\\n    - Details section (date, time, location)\\n    - Why section (event purpose)\\n    - Goals section\\n    - Agenda section\\n    - Speakers section\\n    - Organizers section\\n    - Registration section\\n    - Footer\\n\\n7. Beginner-Friendly Guidance\\nConcepts requiring detailed explanation:\\n- React Context API for state management\\n- Internationalization implementation with translation functions\\n- ShadCN UI component library usage\\n- Tailwind CSS utility-first styling approach\\n- Vite build tool configuration\\n- TypeScript interfaces and types\\n\\nPrerequisite knowledge:\\n- Basic React concepts (components, hooks, JSX)\\n- TypeScript fundamentals\\n- CSS and responsive design principles\\n- Understanding of modern JavaScript (ES6+)\\n- Familiarity with npm package management\\n\\n8. Code Structure Analysis\\nCode structure patterns:\\n- Component composition pattern\\n- Context-based state management\\n- Custom hooks for reusable logic\\n- Separation of concerns between UI components and business logic\\n\\nComponent relationships:\\n- App component wraps all providers (QueryClient, LanguageProvider, TooltipProvider)\\n- Index page imports and composes all section components\\n- Section components use UI components from the ui/ directory\\n- LanguageContext provides translation function (t) and language state to all components\\n\\n9. Data Flow Analysis\\nData pathways:\\n- LanguageContext provides language state and translation function to all components\\n- eventData.ts provides event data to components\\n- Translation system flows from LanguageContext to individual components via the t() function\\n- User interactions (language selection) update context state which propagates to all components\\n\\nCritical data models:\\n- LanguageContextType: Defines the structure of the language context\\n- eventData: Central data object containing all event information\\n- Speaker interface: Defines speaker data structure\\n\\n10. Integration and Extension Points Identification\\nExtension mechanisms:\\n- Language system can be extended with additional languages\\n- Event data can be modified or loaded from external sources\\n- UI components can be customized through Tailwind configuration\\n- Theme can be extended with additional color schemes\\n\\nIntegration points:\\n- Google Maps integration for venue location\\n- Potential registration system integration\\n- Social media sharing capabilities\\n- Analytics integration\\n\\n11. Dependency Analysis\\nExternal dependencies:\\n- React and React DOM: Core UI library\\n- Vite: Build tool and development server\\n- Tailwind CSS: Styling framework\\n- ShadCN UI: Component library built on Radix UI\\n- React Router DOM: Client-side routing\\n- React Query: Data fetching and caching\\n- date-fns: Date manipulation utilities\\n- lucide-react: Icon library\\n\\nInternal component interdependencies:\\n- App depends on all section components and providers\\n- Section components depend on UI components and hooks\\n- UI components depend on utility functions (cn)\\n- All components depend on LanguageContext for translations\\n\\n12. User Workflow Mapping\\nCommon user scenarios:\\n1. User visits site â†’ Language selection â†’ Views event information in selected language\\n2. User navigates through event sections using navbar or scrolling\\n3. User views event details (date, time, location) and clicks to view on map\\n4. User explores agenda, speakers, and organizers\\n5. User registers for event through registration section\\n6. User switches languages at any point to view content in preferred language\\n\\nKey entry points:\\n- Main page (Index) as primary entry point\\n- Direct links to specific sections (agenda, speakers, etc.)\\n- Language switcher for immediate language selection\\n\\n13. Codebase Deep Dive\\nCritical code modules:\\n- LanguageContext.tsx: Manages multilingual functionality with translation system and RTL support\\n- App.tsx: Root application component with providers for routing, internationalization, and state management\\n- Index.tsx: Main page component that composes all sections\\n- eventData.ts: Central data model for event information\\n- ui/ components: ShadCN UI library components built on Radix UI primitives\\n\\nArchitectural patterns:\\n- Component-based architecture with React\\n- Context API for global state management (language, theme)\\n- Atomic design principles in UI components\\n- Custom hooks for reusable logic (use-mobile, use-toast)\\n- Provider pattern for dependency injection\\n\\n6. Feature Hierarchy/Mapping\\n- Core Application\\n  - Internationalization\\n    - Language switching (ar, en, tr)\\n    - RTL layout support\\n    - Translation system\\n  - Responsive Design\\n    - Mobile detection\\n    - Adaptive layouts\\n  - Navigation\\n    - Navbar with language switcher\\n    - Scroll-to-top functionality\\n  - Event Information\\n    - Hero section\\n    - Countdown timer\\n    - Details section (date, time, location)\\n    - Why section (event purpose)\\n    - Goals section\\n    - Agenda section\\n    - Speakers section\\n    - Organizers section\\n    - Registration section\\n    - Footer\\n\\n7. Beginner-Friendly Guidance\\nConcepts requiring detailed explanation:\\n- React Context API for state management\\n- Internationalization implementation with translation functions\\n- ShadCN UI component library usage\\n- Tailwind CSS utility-first styling approach\\n- Vite build tool configuration\\n- TypeScript interfaces and types\\n\\nPrerequisite knowledge:\\n- Basic React concepts (components, hooks, JSX)\\n- TypeScript fundamentals\\n- CSS and responsive design principles\\n- Understanding of modern JavaScript (ES6+)\\n- Familiarity with npm package management\\n\\n8. Code Structure Analysis\\nCode structure patterns:\\n- Component composition pattern\\n- Context-based state management\\n- Custom hooks for reusable logic\\n- Separation of concerns between UI components and business logic\\n\\nComponent relationships:\\n- App component wraps all providers (QueryClient, LanguageProvider, TooltipProvider)\\n- Index page imports and composes all section components\\n- Section components use UI components from the ui/ directory\\n- LanguageContext provides translation function (t) and language state to all components\\n\\n9. Data Flow Analysis\\nData pathways:\\n- LanguageContext provides language state and translation function to all components\\n- eventData.ts provides event data to components\\n- Translation system flows from LanguageContext to individual components via the t() function\\n- User interactions (language selection) update context state which propagates to all components\\n\\nCritical data models:\\n- LanguageContextType: Defines the structure of the language context\\n- eventData: Central data object containing all event information\\n- Speaker interface: Defines speaker data structure\\n\\n10. Integration and Extension Points Identification\\nExtension mechanisms:\\n- Language system can be extended with additional languages\\n- Event data can be modified or loaded from external sources\\n- UI components can be customized through Tailwind configuration\\n- Theme can be extended with additional color schemes\\n\\nIntegration points:\\n- Google Maps integration for venue location\\n- Potential registration system integration\\n- Social media sharing capabilities\\n- Analytics integration\\n\\n11. Dependency Analysis\\nExternal dependencies:\\n- React and React DOM: Core UI library\\n- Vite: Build tool and development server\\n- Tailwind CSS: Styling framework\\n- ShadCN UI: Component library built on Radix UI\\n- React Router DOM: Client-side routing\\n- React Query: Data fetching and caching\\n- date-fns: Date manipulation utilities\\n- lucide-react: Icon library\\n\\nInternal component interdependencies:\\n- App depends on all section components and providers\\n- Section components depend on UI components and hooks\\n- UI components depend on utility functions (cn)\\n- All components depend on LanguageContext for translations\\n\\n12. User Workflow Mapping\\nCommon user scenarios:\\n1. User visits site â†’ Language selection â†’ Views event information in selected language\\n2. User navigates through event sections using navbar or scrolling\\n3. User views event details (date, time, location) and clicks to view on map\\n4. User explores agenda, speakers, and organizers\\n5. User registers for event through registration section\\n6. User switches languages at any point to view content in preferred language\\n\\nKey entry points:\\n- Main page (Index) as primary entry point\\n- Direct links to specific sections (agenda, speakers, etc.)\\n- Language switcher for immediate language selection\\n\\n13.
